n; i++) {\n        wt[i] = wt[i - 1] + bt[i - 1];\n    }\n    printf(&quot;\\nProcess\\tBurst Time\\tWaiting Time\\tTurnaround Time&quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        tat[i] = bt[i] + wt[i];\n        avwt += wt[i];\n        avtat += tat[i];\n        printf(&quot;\\nP[%d]\\t%d\\t\\t%d\\t\\t%d&quot;, i + 1, bt[i], wt[i], tat[i]);\n    }\n    avwt /= n;\n    avtat /= n;\n    printf(&quot;\\n\\nAverage Waiting Time: %d&quot;, avwt);\n    printf(&quot;\\nAverage Turnaround Time: %d&quot;, avtat);\n    return 0;\n}\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<div class=\"highlight highlight-source-c notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n\nint main() {\n    int bt[20], p[20], wt[20], tat[20], n, total_wt = 0, total_tat = 0;\n    float avg_wt, avg_tat;\n    \n    printf(&quot;Enter number of processes: &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;n);\n    \n    printf(&quot;\\nEnter Burst Time:\\n&quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        printf(&quot;p%d: &quot;, i + 1);\n        scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;bt[i]);\n        p[i] = i + 1;\n    }\n    \n    // sort burst time and process number wrt brust time\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n - 1; i++) {\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; n - i - 1; j++) {\n            if (bt[j] &gt; bt[j + 1]) {\n                // Swap burst time\n                int temp = bt[j];\n                bt[j] = bt[j + 1];\n                bt[j + 1] = temp;\n\n                // Swap process number\n                temp = p[j];\n                p[j] = p[j + 1];\n                p[j + 1] = temp;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Calculate waiting time for each process\n    wt[0] = 0;\n    for (int i = 1; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        wt[i] = wt[i - 1] + bt[i - 1];\n        total_wt += wt[i];\n    }\n    \n    // Calculate turnaround time for each process\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        tat[i] = bt[i] + wt[i];\n        total_tat += tat[i];\n    }\n    \n    // Calculate average waiting time and average turnaround time\n    avg_wt = (float)total_wt / n;\n    avg_tat = (float)total_tat / n;\n    \n    // Print results\n    printf(&quot;\\nProcess\\tBurst Time\\tWaiting Time\\tTurnaround Time&quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        printf(&quot;\\np%d\\t\\t%d\\t\\t%d\\t\\t\\t%d&quot;, p[i], bt[i], wt[i], tat[i]);\n    }\n    printf(&quot;\\n\\nAverage Waiting Time=%.2f&quot;, avg_wt);\n    printf(&quot;\\nAverage Turnaround Time=%.2f\\n&quot;, avg_tat);\n    \n    return 0;\n}\n\n\"><pre><span position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n\nint main()\n{\n      int n, time_quantum;\n      int at[10], bt[10], rt[10], wt[10], tat[10];\n      float avg_wt = 0, avg_tat = 0;\n\n      printf(&quot;Enter Total Number of Processes: &quot;);\n      scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;n);\n\n      printf(&quot;Enter Arrival Time and Burst Time for Each Process:\\n&quot;);\n      for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++)\n      {\n            printf(&quot;Process %d:\\n&quot;, i + 1);\n            printf(&quot;Arrival Time: &quot;);\n notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n\nint main() {\n    int bt[20], p[20], wt[20], tat[20], pr[20], n, total = 0, temp, avg_wt, avg_tat;\n\n    printf(&quot;Enter Total Number of Processes: &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;n);\n\n    printf(&quot;\\nEnter Burst Time and Priority for Each Process:\\n&quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        printf(&quot;\\nP[%d]\\n&quot;, i + 1);\n        printf(&quot;Burst Time: &quot;);\n        scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;bt[i]);\n        printf(&quot;Priority: &quot;);\n        scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;pr[i]);\n        p[i] = i + 1;\n    }\n\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        int pos = i;\n        for (int j = i + 1; j &lt; n; j++) {\n            if (pr[j] &lt; pr[pos])\n                pos = j;\n        }\n        temp = pr[i]; pr[i] = pr[pos]; pr[pos] = temp;\n        temp = bt[i]; bt[i] = bt[pos]; bt[pos] = temp;\n        temp = p[i]; p[i] = p[pos]; p[pos] = temp;\n    }\n\n    wt[0] = 0;\n    for (int i = 1; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        wt[i] = 0;\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; i; j++)\n            wt[i] += bt[j];\n        total += wt[i];\n    }\n\n    avg_wt = total / n;\n    total = 0;\n\n    printf(&quot;\\nProcess\\tBurst Time\\tWaiting Time\\tTurnaround Time\\n&quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        tat[i] = bt[i] + wt[i];\n        total += tat[i];\n        printf(&quot;P[%d]\\t%d\\t\\t%d\\t\\t%d\\n&quot;, p[i], bt[i], wt[i], tat[i]);\n    }\n\n    avg_tat = total / n;\n    printf(&quot;\\nAverage Waiting Time: %d&quot;, avg_wt);\n    printf(&quot;\\nAverage Turnaround Time: %d\\n&quot;, avg_tat);\n\n    return 0;\n}\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>\n\n<span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-en\">main</span>() {\n    <span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">bt</span>[<span data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n#include &lt;pthread.h&gt;\n#include &lt;semaphore.h&gt;\n\n#define BUFFER_SIZE 5\n#define MAX_ITEMS 20\n\nint buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];\nint in = 0, out = 0, produced_count = 0, consumed_count = 0;\n\nsem_t mutex, full, empty;\n\nvoid *producer(void *arg) {\n    while (1) {\n        sem_wait(&amp;empty);\n        sem_wait(&amp;mutex);\n        \n        buffer[in] = produced_count + 1;\n        printf(&quot;Produced: %d\\n&quot;, buffer[in]);\n        in = (in + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;\n        produced_count++;\n        \n        sem_post(&amp;mutex);\n        sem_post(&amp;full);\n        \n        if (produced_count == MAX_ITEMS)\n            break;\n    }\n    return NULL;\n}\n\nvoid *consumer(void *arg) {\n    while (1) {\n        sem_wait(&amp;full);\n        sem_wait(&amp;mutex);\n        \n        int item = buffer[out];\n        printf(&quot;Consumed: %d\\n&quot;, item);\n        out = (out + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;\n        consumed_count++;\n        \n        sem_post(&amp;mutex);\n        sem_post(&amp;empty);\n        \n        if (consumed_count == MAX_ITEMS)\n            break;\n    }\n    return NULL;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    pthread_t producer_thread, consumer_thread;\n    \n    sem_init(&amp;mutex, 0, 1);\n    sem_init(&amp;full, 0, 0);\n    sem_init(&amp;empty, 0, BUFFER_SIZE);\n    \n    pthread_create(&amp;producer_thread, NULL, producer, NULL);\n    pthread_create(&amp;consumer_thread, NULL, consumer, NULL);\n    \n    pthread_join(producer_thread, NULL);\n    pthread_join(consumer_thread, NULL);\n    \n    sem_destroy(&amp;mutex);\n    sem_destroy(&amp;full);\n    sem_destroy(&amp;empty);\n    \n    return 0;\n}\n\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;pthread.h&gt;</span>\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;semaphore.h&gt;</span>\n\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#define</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">BUFFER_SIZE</span> 5\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#define</span> <span   <span class=\"pl-k\">while</span> (<span class=\"pl-c1\">1</span>) {\n        <span class=\"pl-en\">sem_wait</span>(<span class=\"pl-c1\">&amp;</span><span class=\"pl-s1\">empty</span>);\n        <span class=\"pl-en\">sem_wait</span>(<span class=\"pl-c1\">&amp;</span><span class=\"pl-s1\">mutex</span>);\n        \n        <span class=\"pl-s1\">buffer</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">in</span>] <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">produced_count</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">+</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">1</span>;\n        <span class=\"pl-en\">printf</span>(<span class=\"pl-s\">\"Produced: %d\\n\"</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">buffer</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">in</span>]);\n        <span class=\"pl-s1\">in</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> (<span <span class=\"pl-c1\">==</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">MAX_ITEMS</span>)\n            <span class=\"pl-k\">break</span>;\n    }\n    <span class=\"pl-k\">return</span> <span <span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">item</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">buffer</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">out</span>];\n        <span class=\"pl-en\">sem_post</span>(<span class=\"pl-c1\">&amp;</span><span class=\"pl-s1\">empty</span>);\n        \n        <span class=\"pl-k\">if</span> (<span class=\"pl-s1\">consumed_count</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">==</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">MAX_ITEMS</span>)\n            <span class=\"pl-k\">break</span>;\n    }\n    <span class=\"pl-k\">return</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">NULL</span>;\n}\n\n<span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-en\">main</span>() {\n    <span class=\"pl-smi\">pthread_t</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">producer_thread</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">consumer_thread</span>;\n    \n    <span class=\"pl-en\">sem_init</span>(<span class=\"pl-c1\">&amp;</span><span class=\"pl-s1\">mutex</span>, <span class=\"pl-c1\">0</span>, <span class=\"pl-c1\">1</span>);\n    <span class=\"pl-en\">sem_init</span>(<span class=\"pl-c1\">&amp;</span><span class=\"pl-s1\">full</span>, <span class=\"pl-c1\">0</span>, <span data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n#define MAX_PROCESSES 10\n#define MAX_RESOURCES 10\n\nint main()\n{\n  int MAX[MAX_PROCESSES][MAX_RESOURCES], alloc[MAX_PROCESSES][MAX_RESOURCES], avail[MAX_RESOURCES];\n  int p, r, i, j, process, count = 0;\n  int completed[MAX_PROCESSES] = {0}; // Array to track completed processes, initialized to 0\n  int safeSequence[MAX_PROCESSES] = {0};\n\n  printf(&quot;Enter the number of processes: &quot;);\n  scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;p);\n\n  printf(&quot;Enter the number of resources: &quot;);\n  scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;r);\n\n  printf(&quot;\\nEnter the max matrix for each process:\\n&quot;);\n  for (i = 0; i &lt; p; i++)\n  {\n    printf(&quot;For process %d: &quot;, i + 1);\n    for (j = 0; j &lt; r; j++)\n      scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;MAX[i][j]);\n  }\n\n  printf(&quot;\\nEnter the allocation for each process:\\n&quot;);\n  for (i = 0; i &lt; p; i++)\n  {\n    printf(&quot;For process %d: &quot;, i + 1);\n    for (j = 0; j &lt; r; j++)\n      scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;alloc[i][j]);\n  }\n\n  printf(&quot;\\nEnter the available resources:\\n&quot;);\n  for (i = 0; i &lt; r; i++)\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;avail[i]);\n\n  do\n  {\n    process = -1; // Initialize process to indicate no process is selected initially\n    // Iterate over each process to find one that can be executed\n    for (i = 0; i &lt; p; i++)\n    {\n      if (!completed[i])\n      {              // If the process is not completed\n        process = i; // Mark the current process as a candidate for execution\n        // Check if the available resources are sufficient to satisfy the needs of this process\n        for (j = 0; j &lt; r; j++)\n        {\n          if (avail[j] &lt; MAX[i][j] - alloc[i][j])\n          {               // If not enough resources available\n            process = -1; // Reset the process selection\n            break;        // Exit the loop for this process\n          }\n        }\n      }\n      if (process != -1) // If a process has been selected for execution\n        break;           // Exit the loop for process selection\n    }\n    if (process != -1)\n    {                                                          // If a process has been selected for execution\n      printf(&quot;\\nProcess %d runs to completion!&quot;, process + 1); // Print the process number\n      safeSequence[count] = i;\n      // Release the allocated resources of the completed process\n      for (j = 0; j &lt; r; j++)\n      {\n        avail[j] += alloc[process][j]; // Return allocated resources to available pool\n        alloc[process][j] = 0;         // Reset the allocation for this process\n        MAX[process][j] = 0;           // Reset the maximum requirement for this process (optional)\n        completed[process] = 1;        // Mark the process as completed\n      }\n      count++;\n    }\n  } while (count != p &amp;&amp; process != -1); // Continue until all processes are completed or deadlock is detected\n\n  if (count == p)\n  {\n    printf(&quot;\\nThe system is in a safe state!\\n&quot;);\n    printf(&quot;Safe Sequence: &lt;&quot;);\n        for (i = 0; i &lt; p - 1; i++)\n            printf(&quot;%d, &quot;, safeSequence[i] +1);\n        printf(&quot;%d&gt;\\n&quot;, safeSequence[p - 1]+ 1);\n    \n  }\n  else\n  {\n    printf(&quot;\\nThe system is in an unsafe state!\\n&quot;);\n  }\n\n  return 0;\n}\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>\n<span 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<div class=\"highlight highlight-source-c notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n\nvoid worstFit(int blocksize[], int m, int processSize[], int n) {\n    int allocation[n];\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        allocation[i] = -1;\n        int wstidx = -1;\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; m; j++) {\n            if (blocksize[j] &gt;= processSize[i] &amp;&amp; (wstidx == -1 || blocksize[wstidx] &lt; blocksize[j])) {\n                wstidx = j;\n            }\n        }\n        if (wstidx != -1) {\n            allocation[i] = wstidx;\n            blocksize[wstidx] -= processSize[i];\n        }\n    }\n    printf(&quot;Process No\\tProcess Size\\tBlock No.\\n&quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        printf(&quot;%d\\t\\t%d\\t\\t&quot;, i + 1, processSize[i]);\n        if (allocation[i] != -1)\n            printf(&quot;%d&quot;, allocation[i] + 1);\n        else\n            printf(&quot;Not Allocated&quot;);\n        printf(&quot;\\n&quot;);\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int blocksize[] = {100, 500, i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        allocation[i] = -1;\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; m; j++) {\n            if (bs[j] &gt;= ps[i] &amp;&amp; (allocation[i] == -1 || bs[allocation[i]] &gt; bs[j])) {\n class=\"highlight highlight-source-c notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n\nvoid firstFit(int blockSizes[], int m, int processSizes[], int n) {\n    int allocation[n];\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        allocation[i] = -1;\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; m; j++) {\n            if (blockSizes[j] &gt;= processSizes[i]) {\n                allocation[i] = j;\n                blockSizes[j] -= processSizes[i];\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    printf(&quot;Process No\\tProcess Size\\tBlock No\\n&quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        printf(&quot;%d\\t\\t%d\\t\\t&quot;, i + 1, processSizes[i]);\n        if (allocation[i] != -1)\n            printf(&quot;%d&quot;, allocation[i] + 1);\n        else\n            printf(&quot;Not Allocated&quot;);\n        printf(&quot;\\n&quot;);\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int blockSizes[] = {100, 500, 200, 300, 50};\n    int processSizes[] = {212, 190, 112, 250, 400};\n    int m = sizeof(blockSizes) / sizeof(blockSizes[0]);\n    int n = sizeof(processSizes) / sizeof(processSizes[0]);\n\n    firstFit(blockSizes, m, processSizes, n);\n    return 0;\n}\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>\n\n<span class=\"pl-smi\">void</span> <span &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n\n#define MAX_FRAMES 10\n#define MAX_PAGES 50\n\nint main() {\n    int reference_string[MAX_PAGES], frames[MAX_FRAMES];\n    int n, num_frames, page_faults = 0, frame_index = 0;\n\n    // Input the number of pages\n    printf(&quot;Enter the number of pages: &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;n);\n\n    // Input the reference string\n    printf(&quot;Enter the reference string: &quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++)\n        scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;reference_string[i]);\n\n    // Input the number of frames\n    printf(&quot;Enter the number of frames: &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;num_frames);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; MAX_FRAMES; i++)\n        frames[i] = -1;\n    // Iterate over the reference string\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        int page_found = 0;\n\n        // Check if page is already in frames\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; num_frames; j++) {\n            if (frames[j] == reference_string[i]) {\n                page_found = 1;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // If page is not in frames, replace the oldest page\n        if (!page_found) {\n            frames[frame_index] = reference_string[i];\n            frame_index = (frame_index + 1) % num_frames;\n            page_faults++;\n        }\n\n        // Print the frames\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; num_frames; j++)\n            printf(&quot;\\t%d&quot;, frames[j]);\n        printf(&quot;\\n&quot;);\n    }\n\n    // Output the number of page faults\n    printf(&quot;\\nThe number of page faults is %d\\n&quot;, page_faults);\n    return 0;\n}\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>\n\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#define</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">MAX_FRAMES</span> &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n#include &lt;stdlib.h&gt;\n\n#define MAX_FRAMES 10\n\nint main() {\n    int reference_string[50], frames[MAX_FRAMES], n, num_frames, page_faults = 0, frame_index = 0;\n    int recent_counter[MAX_FRAMES] = {0};\n\n    // Input the number of pages\n    printf(&quot;Enter the number of pages: &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;n);\n\n    // Input the reference string\n    printf(&quot;Enter the reference string: &quot;);\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++)\n        scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;reference_string[i]);\n\n    // Input the number of frames\n    printf(&quot;Enter the number of frames: &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;num_frames);\n\n    // Initialize frames array to -1 (indicating empty frame)\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; num_frames; i++){\n        frames[i] = -1;\n        recent_counter[i] = -1;\n    }\n\n    // Iterate over the reference string\n    for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {\n        int page_found = 0;\n\n        // Check if page is already in frames\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; num_frames; j++) {\n            if (frames[j] == reference_string[i]) {\n                page_found = 1;\n                recent_counter[j] = i;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // If page is not in frames, replace a page with least recent access\n        if (!page_found) {\n            int lru_frame_index = 0;\n            for (int j = 1; j &lt; num_frames; j++) {\n                if (recent_counter[j] &lt; recent_counter[lru_frame_index])\n                    lru_frame_index = j;\n            }\n            frames[lru_frame_index] = reference_string[i];\n            recent_counter[lru_frame_index] = i;\n            page_faults++;\n        }\n\n        // Print the frames\n        for (int j = 0; j &lt; num_frames; j++)\n            printf(&quot;\\t%d&quot;, frames[j]);\n        printf(&quot;\\n&quot;);\n    }\n\n    // Output the number of page faults\n    printf(&quot;\\nThe data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n#include &lt;string.h&gt;\n#include &lt;stdlib.h&gt;\n\n#define MAX_FILES 10\n#define MAX_FILENAME_LENGTH 10\n#define MAX_DIRECTORY_NAME_LENGTH 10\n\nstruct Directory {\n    char dname[MAX_DIRECTORY_NAME_LENGTH];\n    char fname[MAX_FILES][MAX_FILENAME_LENGTH];\n    int fcnt;\n};\n\nint main() {\n    struct Directory dir;\n    int ch, i;\n    char fname[MAX_FILENAME_LENGTH];\n\n    dir.fcnt = 0;\n\n    printf(&quot;Enter name of directory: &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, dir.dname);\n\n    while (1) {\n        printf(&quot;\\n\\n1. Create File\\t2. Delete File\\t3. Search File\\n4. Display Files\\t5. Exit\\nEnter your choice: &quot;);\n        scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;ch);\n\n        switch (ch) {\n            case 1:\n                printf(&quot;Enter the name of the file: &quot;);\n                scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, dir.fname[dir.fcnt]);\n                dir.fcnt++;\n                break;\n            case 2:\n                printf(&quot;Enter the name of the file: &quot;);\n                scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, fname);\n                for (i = 0; i &lt; dir.fcnt; i++) {\n                    if (strcmp(fname, dir.fname[i]) == 0) {\n                        printf(&quot;File %s is deleted\\n&quot;, fname);\n                        strcpy(dir.fname[i], dir.fname[dir.fcnt - 1]);\n                        dir.fcnt--;\n                        break;\n                    }\n class=\"highlight highlight-source-c notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n#include &lt;string.h&gt;\n#include &lt;stdlib.h&gt;\n\n#define MAX_DIRECTORIES 10\n#define MAX_FILES_PER_DIRECTORY 10\n#define MAX_NAME_LENGTH 30\n\nstruct Directory {\n    char dname[MAX_NAME_LENGTH];\n    char fname[MAX_FILES_PER_DIRECTORY][MAX_NAME_LENGTH];\n    int fcnt;\n};\n\nint main() {\n    struct Directory dir[MAX_DIRECTORIES];\n    int ch, dcnt = 0, i, k;\n    char d[MAX_NAME_LENGTH], f[MAX_NAME_LENGTH];\n\n    while (1) {\n        printf(&quot;\\n\\n1. Create Directory\\t2. Create File\\t3. Delete File\\n4. Search File\\t\\t5. Display\\t6. Exit&quot;);\n        printf(&quot;\\nEnter your choice: &quot;);\n        scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;ch);\n\n        switch (ch) {\n            case 1:\n                printf(&quot;\\nEnter name of directory: &quot;);\n                scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, dir[dcnt].dname);\n                dir[dcnt].fcnt = 0;\n                dcnt++;\n                printf(&quot;Directory created\\n&quot;);\n                break;\n            case 2:\n                printf(&quot;\\nEnter name of the directory: &quot;);\n                scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, d);\n                for (i = 0; i &lt; dcnt; i++) {\n                    if (strcmp(d, dir[i].dname) == 0) {\n                        printf(&quot;Enter name of the file: &quot;);\n                        scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, dir[i].fname[dir[i].fcnt]);\n                        dir[i].fcnt++;\n                        printf(&quot;File created\\n&quot;);\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n                if (i == dcnt)\n                    printf(&quot;Directory %s not found\\n&quot;, d);\n                break;\n            case 3:\n                printf(&quot;\\nEnter name of the directory: &quot;);\n                scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, d);\n                for (i = 0; i &lt; dcnt; i++) {\n                    if (strcmp(d, dir[i].dname) == 0) {\n                        printf(&quot;Enter name of the file: &quot;);\n                        scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, f);\n                        for (k = 0; k &lt; dir[i].fcnt; k++) {\n                            if (strcmp(f, dir[i].fname[k]) == 0) {\n                                printf(&quot;File %s is deleted\\n&quot;, f);\n                                dir[i].fcnt--;\n                                strcpy(dir[i].fname[k], dir[i].fname[dir[i].fcnt]);\n                                break;\n                            }\n                        }\n                        if (k == dir[i].fcnt)\n                            printf(&quot;File %s not found\\n&quot;, f);\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n                if (i == dcnt)\n                    printf(&quot;Directory %s not found\\n&quot;, d);\n                break;\n            case 4:\n                printf(&quot;\\nEnter name of the directory: &quot;);\n                scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, d);\n                for (i = 0; i &lt; dcnt; i++) {\n                    if (strcmp(d, dir[i].dname) == 0) {\n                        printf(&quot;Enter the name of the file: &quot;);\n                        scanf(&quot;%s&quot;, f);\n                        for (k = 0; k &lt; dir[i].fcnt; k++) {\n                            if (strcmp(f, dir[i].fname[k]) == 0) {\n                                printf(&quot;File %s is found\\n&quot;, f);\n                                break;\n                            }\n                        }\n                        if (k == dir[i].fcnt)\n                            printf(&quot;File %s not found\\n&quot;, f);\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n                if (i == dcnt)\n                    printf(&quot;Directory %s not found\\n&quot;, d);\n                break;\n            case 5:\n                if (dcnt == 0)\n                    printf(&quot;\\nNo Directories\\n&quot;);\n                else {\n                    printf(&quot;\\nDirectory\\tFiles\\n&quot;);\n                    for (i = 0; i &lt; dcnt; i++) {\n                        printf(&quot;%s\\t\\t&quot;, dir[i].dname);\n                        for (k = 0; k &lt; dir[i].fcnt; k++)\n                            printf(&quot;%s\\t&quot;, dir[i].fname[k]);\n                        printf(&quot;\\n&quot;);\n                    }\n                }\n                break;\n            case 6:\n                exit(0);\n            default:\n                printf(&quot;Invalid choice\\n&quot;);\n                break;\n        }\n    }\n\n    return 0;\n}\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>\n\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#define</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">MAX_DIRECTORIES</span> 10\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#define</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">MAX_FILES_PER_DIRECTORY</span> 10\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#define</span> <span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-en\">main</span>() {\n    <span class=\"pl-k\">struct</span> <span class=\"pl-smi\">Directory</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">dir</span>[<span class=\"pl-c1\">MAX_DIRECTORIES</span>];\n    <span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">ch</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">dcnt</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">MAX_NAME_LENGTH</span>], <span class=\"pl-s1\">f</span>[<span class=\"pl-c1\">MAX_NAME_LENGTH</span>];\n\n    <span class=\"pl-k\">while</span> (<span class=\"pl-c1\">1</span>) {\n        <span class=\"pl-en\">printf</span>(<span class=\"pl-s\">\"\\n\\n1. Create Directory\\t2. Create File\\t3. Delete File\\n4. Search File\\t\\t5. Display\\t6. <span class=\"pl-c1\">1</span>:\n                <span class=\"pl-en\">printf</span>(<span class=\"pl-s\">\"\\nEnter name of directory: \"</span>);\n                <span // Initialize all blocks as unallocated\n  int num_allocated, start, length, additional_blocks, choice;\n\n  printf(&quot;Enter how many blocks are already allocated: &quot;);\n  scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;num_allocated);\n\n  printf(&quot;Enter the blocks already allocated: &quot;);\n  for (int i = 0; i &lt; num_allocated; i++)\n  {\n    int block;\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;block);\n    allocated[block] = 1; // Mark the block as allocated\n  }\n\n  do\n  {\n    printf(&quot;Enter starting block index and length: &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d %d&quot;, &amp;start, &amp;length);\n\n    additional_blocks = 0;\n\n    if (allocated[start] == 0)\n    {\n      for (int j = start; j &lt; start + length; j++)\n      {\n        if (allocated[j] == 0)\n        {\n          allocated[j] = 1;\n          printf(&quot;%d --------&gt; %d\\n&quot;, j, allocated[j]);\n        }\n        else\n        {\n          printf(&quot;%d Block is already allocated\\n&quot;, j);\n          length++; // Increment length if block is already allocated\n          additional_blocks++;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    else\n    {\n      printf(&quot;%d starting block is already allocated\\n&quot;, start);\n    }\n\n    printf(&quot;Do you want to enter more file? (Yes - 1 / No - 0): &quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;choice);\n  } while (choice == 1);\n\n  return 0;\n}\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>\n<span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span class=\"pl-s\">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>\n\n<span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-en\">main</span>()\n{\n  <span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">allocated</span>[<span class=\"pl-c1\">50</span>] <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> {<span class=\"pl-c1\">0</span>}; <span class=\"pl-c\">// Initialize all blocks as unallocated</span>\n  <span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">num_allocated</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">start</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">length</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">additional_blocks</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">choice</span>;\n\n  <span class=\"pl-en\">printf</span>(<span class=\"pl-s\">\"Enter how many blocks are already allocated: \"</span>);\n  <span class=\"pl-en\">scanf</span>(<span class=\"pl-s\">\"%d\"</span>, <span class=\"pl-c1\">&amp;</span><span class=\"pl-s1\">num_allocated</span>);\n\n  <span class=\"pl-en\">printf</span>(<span class=\"pl-s\">\"Enter the blocks already allocated: \"</span>);\n  <span class=\"pl-k\">for</span> (<span class=\"pl-smi\">int</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">i</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">0</span>; <span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">&lt;</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">start</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">+</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">length</span>; <span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span><span class=\"pl-c1\">++</span>)\n      {\n        <span class=\"pl-k\">if</span> (<span class=\"pl-s1\">allocated</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span>] <span class=\"pl-c1\">==</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">0</span>)\n        {\n          <span class=\"pl-s1\">allocated</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span>] <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">1</span>;\n          <span class=\"pl-en\">printf</span>(<span class=\"pl-s\">\"%d --------&gt; %d\\n\"</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">allocated</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span>]);\n        }\n        <span class=\"pl-k\">else</span>\n        {\n          <span class=\"pl-en\">printf</span>(<span class=\"pl-s\">\"%d Block is already allocated\\n\"</span>, <span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span>);\n          <span class=\"pl-s1\">length</span><span class=\"pl-c1\">++</span>; class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Code</h3><a id=\"user-content-code-16\" class=\"anchor-element\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Code\" href=\"#code-16\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\nint request[50];\nint SIZE;\nint pre;\nint head;\nint uptrack;\nint downtrack;\nstruct max\n{\n    int up;\n    int down;\n} kate[50];\nint dist(int a, int b)\n{\n    if (a &gt; b)\n        return a - b;\n    return b - a;\n}\nvoid sort(int n)\n{\n    int i, j;\n    for (i = 0; i &lt; n - 1; i++)\n    {\n        for (j = 0; j &lt; n - i - 1; j++)\n        {\n            if (request[j] &gt; request[j + 1])\n            {\n                int temp = request[j];\n                request[j] = request[j + 1];\n                request[j + 1] = temp;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    j = 0;\n    i = 0;\n    while (request[i] != head)\n    {\n        kate[j].down = request[i];\n        j++;\n        i++;\n    }\n    downtrack = j;\n    i++;\n    j = 0;\n    while (i &lt; n)\n    {\n        kate[j].up = request[i];\n        j++;\n        i++;\n    }\n    uptrack = j;\n}\nvoid scan(int n)\n{\n    int i;\n    int seekcount = 0;\n    printf(&quot;SEEK SEQUENCE = &quot;);\n    sort(n);\n    if (pre &lt; head)\n    {\n        for (i = 0; i &lt; uptrack; i++)\n        {\n            printf(&quot;%d &quot;, head);\n            seekcount = seekcount + dist(head, kate[i].up);\n            head = kate[i].up;\n        }\n        for (i = downtrack - 1; i &gt; 0; i--)\n        {\n            printf(&quot;%d &quot;, head);\n            seekcount = seekcount + dist(head, kate[i].down);\n            head = kate[i].down;\n        }\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        for (i = downtrack - 1; i &gt;= 0; i--)\n        {\n            printf(&quot;%d &quot;, head);\n            seekcount = seekcount + dist(head, kate[i].down);\n            head = kate[i].down;\n        }\n        for (i = 0; i &lt; uptrack - 1; i++)\n        {\n            printf(&quot;%d &quot;, head);\n            seekcount = seekcount + dist(head, kate[i].up);\n            head = kate[i].up;\n        }\n    }\n    printf(&quot; %d\\nTOTAL DISTANCE :%d&quot;, head, seekcount);\n}\nint main()\n{\n    int n, i;\n    printf(&quot;ENTER THE DISK SIZE :\\n&quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;SIZE);\n    printf(&quot;ENTER THE NO OF REQUEST SEQUENCE :\\n&quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;n);\n    printf(&quot;ENTER THE REQUEST SEQUENCE :\\n&quot;);\n    for (i = 0; i &lt; n; i++)\n        scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;request[i]);\n    printf(&quot;ENTER THE CURRENT HEAD :\\n&quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;head);\n    request[n] = head;\n    request[n + 1] = SIZE - 1;\n    request[n + 2] = 0;\n    printf(&quot;ENTER THE PRE REQUEST :\\n&quot;);\n    scanf(&quot;%d&quot;, &amp;pre);\n    scan(n + 3);\n}\n\"><pre><span class=\"pl-k\">#include</span> <span      <span class=\"pl-s1\">request</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">+</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">1</span>] <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">0</span>;\n    <span class=\"pl-k\">while</span> (<span class=\"pl-s1\">request</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">i</span>] <span        <span class=\"pl-s1\">i</span><span class=\"pl-c1\">++</span>;\n    }\n    <span class=\"pl-s1\">uptrack</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">j</span>;\n}\n<span         <span class=\"pl-s1\">head</span> <span class=\"pl-c1\">=</span> <span class=\"pl-s1\">kate</span>[<span class=\"pl-s1\">i</span>].<span class=\"pl-c1\">down</span>;\n        }\n    }\n
